<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a> (321)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gilīk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*galīkaz</i>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">alike</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>right
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeker.html>zeker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> convinced that he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>right</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>truth
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>hebt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>You are <b>correct</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gelijkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>equal; like; alike; similar
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It's all the <b>same</b> to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>Juist</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> ?</i>
<dl><dd>Just <b>like</b> that ?</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pertaining to rank, value, worth etc.</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> equal, equivalent
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:iedereen.html>Iedereen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>Everybody <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>equal</b> before the law.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***gelijken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelijken.html>gelijken</a> (14244)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geliken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gilīkon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*galīkōną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijken.html>lijken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelijken.html>gelijken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to resemble [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span>]</li></ol>

<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen_2"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>

***geloof.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloof</a> (281)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelove.html>gelove</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gelôve</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gilōvo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*galaubô</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloof</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloven.html>geloven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloofje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>belief, conviction.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> faith, religion.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The genitive form of the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geloofs.html>geloofs</a></i>. Of its alternative form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:gelove.html>gelove</a></i> it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geloven.html>geloven</a></i> or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> geloves</i>. In Dutch, the genitive <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not commonly used outside of fixed expressions and literary language, but can be frequently encountered in early modern Dutch texts.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">belief<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> conviction</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overtuiging.html>overtuiging</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:godsdienst.html>godsdienst</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:religie.html>religie</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloof</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloven.html>geloven</a></i></span></li>

***geloven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geloven.html>geloven</a> (379)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gelôven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gilōven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*galaubijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to believe, to hold valuable or pleasing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloven.html>geloven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to believe, to hold a belief [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> <span>(object)</span></span> = in]</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to believe, to be convinced by
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:geloofde.html>Geloofde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>Did</a> he <b>believe</b> us?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:geloven.html>geloven</a></b>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geluc</i>, further origin unknown. Found only in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:West Germanic languages">West Germanic</a></span>.  More at <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Glück</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">joy, bliss, luck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>luck, good luck</li>
<li>happiness</li></ol>

***gelukkig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a> (466)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geluckig</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geluk.html>geluk</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkiger.html>gelukkiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkigst.html>gelukkigst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>happy</li>
<li>pleased, satisfied</li>
<li>lucky</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Indefinite adjectives describing people often remain uninflected, if they express a personal quality. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not stylistically neutral, but <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a formal, rhetorical or poetic <a href = vnd.unilang:ring.html>ring</a> to it, and can occasionally distinguish literal meanings of an adjective from a more figurative one. Furthermore, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> only done with some nouns, not all. Hence, besides the regularly inflected "<a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkige.html>gelukkige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>", the uninflected "<a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>" can also be encountered.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>luckily</li>
<li>thankfully</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li>in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> tevredene <a href = vnd.unilang:toestand.html>toestand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voelen.html>voelen</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>"<a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>Veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergissen.html>vergissen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:maakt.html>maakt</a>" <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd>
<dd><span style="color:0060ff;font-weight: bold;">▸</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hemel.html>hemel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zomer.html>zomer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verjaagt.html>verjaagt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zuur.html>zuur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zong.html>zong</a> Charles Trenet <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a>: '<a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>Wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></b>, Route <a href = vnd.unilang:nationale.html>Nationale</a> 7.'</i><sup id="cite_ref-Route_Nationale_7,_leuker_dan_de_Route_du_Soleil_3-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Route_Nationale_7,_leuker_dan_de_Route_du_Soleil-3"> | 3 | </a></sup></dd></dl></li></ol>

***gemaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemaal.html>gemaal</a> (75800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gemahl</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">gemahele</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">gimahalo</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gemahela</i>, which didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> persist into Middle Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemaal.html>gemaal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemaal.html>gemaals</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemalen.html>gemalen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemaal.html>gemaaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemalin.html>gemalin</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in titles</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A consort.</li>
<li>A husband.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gemael</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:malen.html>malen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemaal.html>gemaal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemalen.html>gemalen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemaal.html>gemaaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The act or process of grinding (of grain).</li>
<li>A pump house, mill, pumping-engine or several of these used for draining polders.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gemaal.html>gemaal</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <i>(<a href = vnd.unilang:formeel.html>formeel</a>)</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:echtgenoot.html>echtgenoot</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></li>
<li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span> <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(waterstaat)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:installatie.html>installatie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:overtollig.html>overtollig</a> water <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> polder uitmaalt</li></ol>

***gember.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gember.html>gember</a> (28206)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gingebare</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gingiber</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">zingiber</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ζιγγίβερις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zingíberis</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shauraseni_Prakrit" class="extiw" title="w:Shauraseni Prakrit">Sauraseni Prakrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="psu">सिङ्गबेर</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="psu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">siṅgabera</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gemêen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gimēni</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gamainiz</i>.

</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">somewhat  dated  outside set phrases</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> common, shared, communal</li></ol>

<p>Early 19th century. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemeenschap.html>gemeenschap</a> (2736)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeenschap.html>gemeenschap</a></i>, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gemeinschaft</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Gemeenschop</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeen.html>gemeen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-schap</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemeente.html>gemeente</a> (6212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gemeende</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gimēnitha</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gamainiz</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*-iþō</i>. Corresponds to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeen.html>gemeen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">common</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeente.html>gemeente</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeenten.html>gemeenten</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeentes.html>gemeentes</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeente.html>gemeentetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>municipality, commune</li>
<li>congregation</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In the Netherlands and Belgium, a municipality (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeente.html>gemeente</a></i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> part of a province (<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:provincie.html>provincie</a></i>), and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> analogous to a county. Villages and small <a href = vnd.unilang:towns.html>towns</a> in a municipality are called <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dorpen.html>dorpen</a></i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plaatsen.html>plaatsen</a></i>. Larger <a href = vnd.unilang:towns.html>towns</a> and cities are called <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steden.html>steden</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeenschap.html>gemeenschap</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">community</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeen.html>gemeen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">common</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-zaam</i>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> familiar, intimate</li>

<li>Of speech: colloquial, informal
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeenzame.html>gemeenzame</a></b> taalgebruik.</i>  |  Informal language; everyday speech.</dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeenzame.html>gemeenzame</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitdrukking.html>uitdrukking</a>.</i>  |  A common expression.</dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeenzaam.html>Gemeenzaam</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:klinken.html>klinken</a>.</i>  |  To sound familiar.</dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeen.html>gemeen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">common</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a></i> (superlative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">good</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).

<p>Verbal noun of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:missen.html>missen</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemis.html>gemis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>lack, absence; in particular one that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> strongly felt emotionally
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gemis.html>gemis</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> klopboormachine <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> werkbank <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>groot</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gemis.html>gemis</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>absence</b> of a percussion drill on the workbench <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a large <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaping.html>gaping</a> hole in</b> her <b>heart</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>loss, especially a very emotional loss</li></ol>
